class=\"story-meta\">\n                                                                            <h1 class=\"story-heading interactive-headline\" itemprop=\"headline\">Highlights: Georgia Special Election</h1>\n            \n            <div class=\"story-meta-footer interactive-meta-footer\">\n                                 <p class=\"interactive-leadin summary\">\n            <span class=\"summary-text\">Here\u2019s how we analyzed Georgia\u2019s special election through about 11 p.m. Eastern on Tuesday, which the Democrat Jon Ossoff cast as a referendum on President Trump. Keep watching <strong><a href=\"http://www.nytimes.com/elections/results/georgia-house-special-election-district-6\">live results</a></strong> as they come in, and <strong><a href=\"https://www.nytimes.com/newsletters/morning-briefing\">sign up for our email newsletter</a></strong>.</span>\n    \n        \t\t\t        \t<time class=\"dateline\" datetime=\"2017-04-18\" itemprop=\"dateModified\" content=\"2017-04-18\">APRIL 18, 2017</time>\n\t    \t                                </p>\n            </div><!-- close story-meta-footer -->\n\n        </div><!-- close story-meta -->\n        </header>\n    <div id=\"georgia-special-election-live\" class=\"interactive-graphic\">\n                <link rel=\"stylesheet\" href=\"https://int.nyt.com/apps/chatblog/assets/public/main-240235699db7e6c5b42ae1518be1039a0e0a1b828ef1401b597f338fc2783227.css\"/>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"live-chat waiting-for-scroll touch-move-enabled archived\">\n  <p id=\"live-chat-sticky-intro\" class=\"sticky-intro chat-description\"></p>\n  <div class=\"posts-wrapper\">\n    <ol id=\"posts\" class=\"posts\" data-total=\"357\">\n      \n      \n        \n        <li id=\"message-18606\" data-guid=\"18606\" class=\"post post-moderator user-type-nyt type-basic author-2 has-headshot avatar-color-5 author-id-3636\" data-published-at=\"2017-04-18 18:41:36 -0400\">\n  <div class=\"post-meta\">\n    <div class=\"post-author\">\n      \n        <img class=\"post-author-avatar\" src=\"https://static01.nyt.com/images/2017/04/17/us/politics/alex-burns/alex-burns-thumbStandard.jpg\" />\n      \n      \n      <h3 class=\"post-author-name\">Alex Burns</h3>\n      <h4 class=\"post-author-title\">Political Reporter</h4>\n    </div>\n    <time class=\"post-timestamp\" datetime=\"2017-04-18T18:41:36\" title=\"April 18,  6:41 PM ET\">\n      <span class=\"date\">April 18, </span>\n       6:41 PM ET\n    </time>\n  </div>\n  <div class=\"post-body\"><p>Happy special election day, everyone! We&rsquo;re going to be watching the results of a very unusual congressional race in Georgia, where Democrats are trying to snatch away the House seat once held by Tom Price, President Trump\u2019s health secretary.  </p>\n\n<p>Both parties have pumped millions into the election, and it\u2019s become a significant test of the Republican Party\u2019s strength in a red-leaning district. Most polling locations close at 7 p.m., and we should get the earliest results soon after that. <div class=\"story-unfurl source-nyt\">      <a href=\"https://www.nytimes.com/2017/04/18/us/politics/georgia-special-election-jon-ossoff.html\" target=\"_blank\" class=\"story-link\">            <figure id=\"media-100000005049495\" class=\"photo class=\"unfurl-meta\">     <a href=\"https://www.nytimes.com/2017/04/18/us/politics/georgia-special-election-jon-ossoff.html\" target=\"_blank\" class=\"story-link\">       <h4 class=\"unfurl-heading\">Will Georgia\u2019s Special Election Show an Anti-Trump Tide?</h4>     </a>            <p class=\"unfurl-summary\">Liberals are rallying behind the anti-Trump candidate, Jon Ossoff, but Republicans in a conservative district believe they will triumph in a June runoff.</p>          <div class=\"unfurl-credit\">       <img class=\"author-image\" src=\"https://int.nyt.com/newsgraphics/slack/assets/nyticon.png\">       <p class=\"author-name\">The New York Times</p>     </div>   </div> </div> </p>\n</div>\n</li>\n      \n        \n        <li id=\"message-18616\" data-guid=\"18616\" class=\"post post-moderator user-type-nyt type-basic author-2 has-headshot avatar-color-5 author-id-3636\" data-published-at=\"2017-04-18 18:53:38 -0400\">\n  <div class=\"post-meta\">\n    <div class=\"post-author\">\n      \n        <img class=\"post-author-avatar\" src=\"https://static01.nyt.com/images/2017/04/17/us/politics/alex-burns/alex-burns-thumbStandard.jpg\" />\n      \n      \n      <h3 class=\"post-author-name\">Alex Burns</h3>\n      <h4 class=\"post-author-title\">Political Reporter</h4>\n    </div>\n    <time class=\"post-timestamp\" datetime=\"2017-04-18T18:53:38\" title=\"April 18,  6:53 PM ET\">\n      <span class=\"date\">April 18, </span>\n       6:53 PM ET\n    </time>\n  </div>\n  <div class=\"post-body\"><p>It\u2019s a quirky election: You have one major Democrat, Jon Ossoff, a 30-year-old filmmaker who has never held public office, competing in an open primary against four significant Republican candidates. If no one gets a majority, the top two finishers advance to a June runoff. So the big question this evening is: Can Ossoff get to 50 percent?</p>\n\n<p>No Democrat has come close to winning the district in a long time, but the race has unfolded under tough conditions for Republicans, and they\u2019re genuinely concerned that anti-Trump fervor could cause an upset. You can follow the results as they come in here. <div class=\"story-unfurl source-nyt\">      <a href=\"http://www.nytimes.com/elections/results/georgia-house-special-election-district-6\" target=\"_blank\" class=\"story-link\">        </a>      <div class=\"unfurl-meta\">     <a href=\"http://www.nytimes.com/elections/results/georgia-house-special-election-district-6\" target=\"_blank\" class=\"story-link\">       <h4 class=\"unfurl-heading\">Live Election Results: Georgia&rsquo;s Sixth Congressional District</h4>     </a>            <p class=\"unfurl-summary\">Maps and results in a U.S. House race where Jon Ossoff, a young Democrat, tries to win a vacant seat.</p>          <div class=\"unfurl-credit\">       <img class=\"author-image\" src=\"https://int.nyt.com/newsgraphics/slack/assets/nyticon.png\">       <p class=\"author-name\">The New York Times</p>     </div>   </div> </div> </p>\n</div>\n</li>\n      \n        \n        <li id=\"message-18631\" data-guid=\"18631\" class=\"post post-moderator user-type-nyt type-basic author-1 has-headshot avatar-color-2 author-id-3633\" data-published-at=\"2017-04-18 18:59:35 -0400\">\n  <div class=\"post-meta\">\n    <div class=\"post-author\">\n      \n        <img class=\"post-author-avatar\" src=\"https://static01.nyt.com/images/2016/07/15/us/chat-nate-cohn/chat-nate-cohn-thumbStandard-v2.png\" />\n      \n      \n      <h3 class=\"post-author-name\">Nate Cohn</h3>\n      <h4 class=\"post-author-title\">Reporter with The Upshot</h4>\n    </div>\n    <time class=\"post-timestamp\" datetime=\"2017-04-18T18:59:35\" title=\"April 18,  6:59 PM ET\">\n      <span class=\"date\">April 18, </span>\n       6:59 PM ET\n    </time>\n  </div>\n  <div class=\"post-body\"><p>I think quirky is a great word for it, Alex. It&rsquo;s a district where Trump won by 1.5 points, but Romney won by 23. So there&rsquo;s a lot of room to debate just how safe the seat should really be for the Republicans.</p>\n</div>\n</li>\n      \n        \n        <li id=\"message-18632\" data-guid=\"18632\" class=\"post post-moderator user-type-nyt type-basic author-1 has-headshot avatar-color-2 author-id-3633\" data-published-at=\"2017-04-18 19:03:03 -0400\">\n  <div class=\"post-meta\">\n    <div class=\"post-author\">\n      \n        <img class=\"post-author-avatar\" src=\"https://static01.nyt.com/images/2016/07/15/us/chat-nate-cohn/chat-nate-cohn-thumbStandard-v2.png\" />\n      \n      \n      <h3 class=\"post-author-name\">Nate Cohn</h3>\n      <h4 class=\"post-author-title\">Reporter with The Upshot</h4>\n    </div>\n    <time class=\"post-timestamp\" datetime=\"2017-04-18T19:03:03\" title=\"April 18,  7:03 PM ET\">\n      <span class=\"date\">April 18, </span>\n       7:03 PM ET\n    </time>\n  </div>\n  <div class=\"post-body\"><p>The only thing I feel confident about is that Jon Ossoff, the Democrat, likely fared very well in the early vote. The first results should look quite good for him, and then we&rsquo;ll have to wait a while to see just how well he fared among voters who cast their ballots today.</p>\n</div>\n</li>\n      \n        \n        <li id=\"message-18634\" data-guid=\"18634\" class=\"post post-moderator user-type-nyt type-basic author-2 has-headshot avatar-color-5 author-id-3636\" data-published-at=\"2017-04-18 19:03:10 -0400\">\n  <div class=\"post-meta\">\n    <div class=\"post-author\">\n      \n        <img class=\"post-author-avatar\" src=\"https://static01.nyt.com/images/2017/04/17/us/politics/alex-burns/alex-burns-thumbStandard.jpg\" />\n      \n      \n      <h3 class=\"post-author-name\">Alex Burns</h3>\n      <h4 class=\"post-author-title\">Political Reporter</h4>\n    </div>\n    <time class=\"post-timestamp\" datetime=\"2017-04-18T19:03:10\" title=\"April 18,  7:03 PM ET\">\n      <span class=\"date\">April 18, </span>\n       7:03 PM ET\n    </time>\n  </div>\n  <div class=\"post-body\"><p>To your point about the nature of the seat: The district isn&rsquo;t really a good approximation of the country as a whole. It&rsquo;s more affluent, more conservative, etc. What it does approximate reasonably well is the traditional Republican political coalition. So one thing we might find out tonight is how good a job Trump is doing of holding on to traditional, Romney-type Republican voters.</p>\n</div>\n</li>\n      \n        \n          <li class=\"d-ad-wrapper\" data-idx=\"1\">\n            <div class=\"ad-placeholder\"></div>\n          </li>\n        \n        <li id=\"message-18635\" data-guid=\"18635\" class=\"post post-moderator user-type-nyt type-basic author-0 has-headshot avatar-color-7 author-id-3630\" data-published-at=\"2017-04-18 19:03:11 -0400\">\n  <div class=\"post-meta\">\n    <div class=\"post-author\">\n      \n        <img class=\"post-author-avatar\" src=\"https://static01.nyt.com/images/2016/07/15/us/chat-maggie-haberman/chat-maggie-haberman-thumbStandard-v2.png\" />\n      \n      \n      <h3 class=\"post-author-name\">Maggie Haberman</h3>\n      <h4 class=\"post-author-title\">White House Correspondent</h4>\n    </div>\n    <time class=\"post-timestamp\" datetime=\"2017-04-18T19:03:11\" title=\"April 18,  7:03 PM ET\">\n      <span class=\"date\">April 18, </span>\n       7:03 PM ET\n    </time>\n  </div>\n  <div class=\"post-body\"><p>Hi all. I think it&rsquo;s hard to generalize a broader lesson.</p>\n</div>\n</li>\n      \n        \n        <li id=\"message-18640\" data-guid=\"18640\" class=\"post post-moderator user-type-nyt type-basic   <h3 class=\"post-author-name\">Alex Burns</h3>\n      <h4 class=\"post-author-title\">Political Reporter</h4>\n    </div>\n    <time class=\"post-timestamp\" datetime=\"2017-04-18T19:13:13\"  <h4 class=\"post-author-title\">White House Correspondent</h4>\n    </div>\n    <time class=\"post-timestamp\" datetime=\"2017-04-18T19:13:28\" title=\"April 18,  7:13 PM ET\">\n      <span id=\"message-18650\" data-guid=\"18650\" class=\"post post-moderator user-type-nyt type-basic author-2 has-headshot avatar-color-5 author-id-3636\" data-published-at=\"2017-04-18 19:14:43 -0400\">\n  <div class=\"post-meta\">\n    <div class=\"post-author\">\n      \n        <img class=\"post-author-avatar\" class=\"post-author-title\">Political Reporter</h4>\n    </div>\n    <time class=\"post-timestamp\" datetime=\"2017-04-18T19:14:43\" title=\"April 18,  7:14 PM ET\">\n      <span class=\"date\">April 18, </span>\n       7:14 PM ET\n    </time>\n  </div>\n  <div class=\"post-body\"><p>I would have guessed that a bunch of conservative, college-educated, white Republicans would be inclined to fault the president, because so many disliked him as a candidate last year. And they don&rsquo;t love him. But there was as much Paul Ryan bashing as Trump bashing, and most of all, a lot of heavy sighing and eye-rolling.</p>\n</div>\n</li>\n      \n        \n        <li id=\"message-18651\" data-guid=\"18651\" class=\"post post-moderator user-type-nyt type-basic author-0 has-headshot avatar-color-7 author-id-3630\" data-published-at=\"2017-04-18 19:15:19 -0400\">\n  <div class=\"post-meta\">\n    <div class=\"post-author\">\n      \n        <img class=\"post-author-avatar\" src=\"https://static01.nyt.com/images/2016/07/15/us/chat-maggie-haberman/chat-maggie-haberman-thumbStandard-v2.png\" />\n      \n      \n      <h3 class=\"post-author-name\">Maggie Haberman</h3>\n      <h4 class=\"post-author-title\">White House Correspondent</h4>\n    </div>\n    <time class=\"post-timestamp\" datetime=\"2017-04-18T19:15:19\" title=\"April 18,  7:15 PM ET\">\n      <span class=\"date\">April 18, </span>\n       7:15 PM ET\n    </time>\n  </div>\n  <div class=\"post-body\"><p>So, what, to your mind, constitutes the threshold for measuring how hostile the environment is for Republicans more broadly? So sorry I took so long. One of the horrible things about Georgia-6, the district I grew up in, is the terrible public transportation. Well, now I&rsquo;m in Washington, where the Metro periodically comes crashing to a halt and you have to cobble together a trip home by foot and bus. So here I am.</p>\n</div>\n</li>\n      \n        \n        <li id=\"message-18672\" data-guid=\"18672\" class=\"post post-moderator user-type-nyt type-basic author-2 has-headshot avatar-color-5 author-id-3636\" data-published-at=\"2017-04-18 19:27:22 -0400\">\n  <div class=\"post-meta\">\n    <div class=\"post-author\">\n      \n        <img class=\"post-author-avatar\" src=\"https://static01.nyt.com/images/2017/04/17/us/politics/alex-burns/alex-burns-thumbStandard.jpg\" />\n      \n      \n      <h3 class=\"post-author-name\">Alex Burns</h3>\n      <h4 class=\"post-author-title\">Political Reporter</h4>\n    </div>\n    <time class=\"post-timestamp\" datetime=\"2017-04-18T19:27:22\" title=\"April 18,  7:27 PM ET\">\n      <span class=\"date\">April 18, </span>\n       7:27 PM ET\n    </time>\n  </div>\n  <div class=\"post-body\"><p>Even WMATA can&rsquo;t keep a good man down &hellip;</p>\n</div>\n</li>\n      \n        \n        <li id=\"message-18673\" data-guid=\"18673\" class=\"post post-moderator user-type-nyt type-basic author-3 has-headshot avatar-color-5 author-id-3644\" data-published-at=\"2017-04-18 19:27:43 -0400\">\n  <div class=\"post-meta\">\n    <div class=\"post-author\">\n      \n        <img class=\"post-author-avatar\" src=\"https://static01.nyt.com/images/2017/04/17/us/politics/jonathan-weisman/jonathan-weisman-thumbStandard-v2.jpg\" />\n      \n      \n      <h3 class=\"post-author-name\">Jonathan Weisman</h3>\n      <h4 class=\"post-author-title\">Deputy Editor</h4>\n    </div>\n    <time class=\"post-timestamp\" datetime=\"2017-04-18T19:27:43\" title=\"April 18,  7:27 PM ET\">\n      <span class=\"date\">April 18, </span>\n       7:27 PM ET\n    </time>\n  </div>\n  <div class=\"post-body\"><p>So, my thoughts on this race: Wow, there hasn&rsquo;t been this much excitement in a House race north of Atlanta since, well&hellip;    <h4 class=\"post-author-title\">Deputy Editor</h4>\n    </div>\n    <time class=\"post-timestamp\" datetime=\"2017-04-18T19:39:12\" title=\"April 18,  7:39 PM ET\">\n      <span the 50 percent mark rather than who the runner-up is. Handel is well ahead of all the other Republicans. Which is really striking, given how well funded some of her opponents were.</p>\n</div>\n</li>\n      \n        \n        <li id=\"message-18966\" data-guid=\"18966\" class=\"post post-moderator user-type-nyt type-basic author-0 has-headshot avatar-color-7 author-id-3630\" data-published-at=\"2017-04-18 21:43:41 -0400\">\n  <div class=\"post-meta\">\n    <div class=\"post-author\">\n      \n        <img class=\"post-author-avatar\" src=\"https://static01.nyt.com/images/2016/07/15/us/chat-maggie-haberman/chat-maggie-haberman-thumbStandard-v2.png\" />\n      \n      \n      <h3 class=\"post-author-name\">Maggie Haberman</h3>\n      <h4 class=\"post-author-title\">White House Correspondent</h4>\n    </div>\n    <time class=\"post-timestamp\" datetime=\"2017-04-18T21:43:41\" title=\"April 18,  9:43 PM ET\">\n      <span class=\"date\">April 18, </span>\n       9:43 PM ET\n    </time>\n  </div>\n  <div class=\"post-body\"><p>To what do you attribute her success here?</p>\n</div>\n</li>\n      \n        \n        <li id=\"message-18967\" data-guid=\"18967\" class=\"post post-moderator user-type-nyt type-basic author-2 has-headshot avatar-color-5 author-id-3636\" data-published-at=\"2017-04-18 21:43:52 -0400\">\n  <div class=\"post-meta\">\n    <div class=\"post-author\">\n      \n        <img class=\"post-author-avatar\" src=\"https://static01.nyt.com/images/2017/04/17/us/politics/alex-burns/alex-burns-thumbStandard.jpg\" />\n      \n      \n      <h3 class=\"post-author-name\">Alex Burns</h3>\n      <h4 class=\"post-author-title\">Political Reporter</h4>\n    </div>\n    <time class=\"post-timestamp\" datetime=\"2017-04-18T21:43:52\" title=\"April 18,  9:43 PM ET\">\n      <span class=\"date\">April 18, </span>\n       9:43 PM ET\n    </time>\n  </div>\n  <div class=\"post-body\"><p>You could see shuffling around between third and fifth place, but right now Dan Moody, a self-funded candidate backed by Senator David Perdue, is dead last among the major candidates. And Bob Gray, the favorite of the Club for Growth, is barely ahead of him.</p>\n</div>\n</li>\n      \n        \n        <li id=\"message-18968\" data-guid=\"18968\" class=\"post post-moderator       <img class=\"post-author-avatar\" src=\"https://static01.nyt.com/images/2017/04/17/us/politics/alex-burns/alex-burns-thumbStandard.jpg\" />\n      \n      \n      <h3
